## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology (population dynamics / growth models)
**Analysis**: The target dP_dt with variables time t and population size P indicates a continuous-time population dynamics ODE where growth rate depends on current abundance (density dependence) and possibly explicit time-varying forcing. Common structures include exponential growth, density-limited growth, Allee effects, harvesting, and seasonal/environmental modulation of growth parameters.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Exponential (Malthusian) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (density-independent per-capita growth)
- Time-varying intrinsic growth: dP_dt = (c0 + c1 * t) * P (trend in per-capita growth due to environment/management)
- Quadratic density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P**2 (crowding/competition causing nonlinear mortality)
- General polynomial growth law: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (empirical density effects beyond quadratic)
- Gompertz growth (continuous): dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (logarithmic density feedback; approach to carrying capacity)
- Theta-logistic (generalized density limitation): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (flexible crowding strength via exponent c2)
- Richards-type generalized logistic derivative: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2)**c3 (adjustable asymmetry/shape of approach to capacity)
- Strong Allee effect with crowding: dP_dt = c0 * P * (c1 * P - 1) * (1 - c2 * P) (low-density suppression plus high-density limitation)
- Weak Allee effect (per-capita growth increases with P at low density): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * P) (facilitation at low P with eventual crowding)
- Linear harvesting/extra mortality: dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P**2 - c2 * P (removal proportional to abundance)
- Constant-yield harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P**2 - c2 (fixed quota removal independent of P)
- Seasonally forced growth (multiplicative forcing): dP_dt = (c0 + c1 * sin(c2 * t + c3)) * P (periodic environment affecting intrinsic growth)
- Seasonally forced density limitation: dP_dt = (c0 + c1 * sin(c2 * t + c3)) * P * (1 - c4 * P) (periodic r with crowding)
- Pulse/relaxation forcing via exponential time trend: dP_dt = (c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) * P - c3 * P**2 (transient environmental shift affecting growth)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope ŌåÆ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects ŌåÆ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay ŌåÆ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior ŌåÆ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects ŌåÆ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Per-capita growth rate interpretation: if dP_dt has a factor P (i.e., dP_dt = P * f(t,P)), then f is the per-capita growth rate; checking whether f decreases with P diagnoses density dependence.
- Carrying-capacity-like behavior: factors such as (1 - c * P) or sign changes in dP_dt vs P imply an equilibrium P* Ōēł 1/c where growth switches from positive to negative.
- Crowding/competition signature: a negative P**2 term (or higher powers) indicates increasing marginal mortality/competition with density; higher powers often model stronger-than-quadratic crowding.
- Allee effect signature: a low-density root like (c * P - 1) implies negative growth below a threshold P Ōēł 1/c, producing extinction vs persistence bistability.
- Asymmetric approach to equilibrium: logarithmic feedback (P * log(c/P)) yields fast early growth with a progressively slowing approach (Gompertz-like), often fitting biological growth better than symmetric forms.
- Time-dependent environment/management: coefficients that vary with t (c0 + c1*t, exp(c*t), sin(c*t)) represent nonstationary conditions; periodic terms suggest seasonality.
- Harvesting/removal identification: additive negative terms independent of P suggest constant-yield harvest, while negative terms proportional to P suggest proportional harvest/extra mortality.
- Multiple equilibria from factorized forms: products like P*(c1*P-1)*(1-c2*P) indicate equilibria at P=0 and at the roots; stability can often be inferred from sign changes across roots.
- Nonlinear density dependence flexibility: exponents on P in limiting terms (e.g., (c*P)**theta) allow fitting either sharp (theta>1) or gradual (theta<1) saturation in growth limitation.

GT Equivalence Verification (BPG19)
============================================================
GT: c0*(c1 - P/c2)*P + c3*P/t**c4
Candidate formulas: 83

GT (fixed) simplifies to a polynomial in \(P\) plus a separable \(P/t^{\alpha}\) term:
\[
0.4205670824\,(1-P/84.41334764)\,P \;+\; 0.4205670824\,\frac{P}{t^{2.594538327}}
\]
Expand the first part:
\[
0.4205670824\,P \;-\;\frac{0.4205670824}{84.41334764}P^2 \;+\; 0.4205670824\,P\,t^{-2.594538327}.
\]
So GT has exactly these three components:
- a \(P^2\) term with coefficient \(-0.4205670824/84.41334764\),
- a \(P\) term with coefficient \(+0.4205670824\),
- a \(P\cdot t^{-2.594538327}\) term with coefficient \(+0.4205670824\),
and **no other dependence** (no logs, trig, exp, Max, rational-in-\(P\), etc.).

Now check candidates: any extra functional form must be zeroed out by setting its prefactor to 0; and the remaining terms must be able to realize \(P^2\), \(P\), and \(P t^{-2.5945}\).

1. \(P^2c0 + Pc1 + Pc2 t^{c3} + P^{c4}c5\log(c6 t+1)\cos(\cdot)\): can zero last term via \(c5=0\). Then need \(Pc2 t^{c3}=0.4205\,P t^{-2.5945}\) achievable with \(c2=0.4205, c3=-2.5945\). Also set \(c0, c1\) to match \(P^2\) and \(P\). **Matches possible.**

2. Same but extra \(c4\exp(Pc5)\sin(\cdot)\): must set \(c4=0\) to remove non-polynomial/non-separable \(P\) dependence. Remaining \(Pc2 t^{c3}\) can match \(P t^{-2.5945}\). **Matches possible.**

3. Extra \(P^{c4}c5\sin(\cdot)\): set \(c5=0\). Remaining can match. **Matches possible.**

4. Has \(Pc2(c3+t)^{c4}\) and \(\log(Pc6+1)\sin(\cdot)\). Need \(P t^{-2.5945}\) but only \((c3+t)^{c4}\). If set \(c3=0\), becomes \(P c2 t^{c4}\) which can match with \(c4=-2.5945\). Kill log-sin via \(c5=0\). **Matches possible.**

5. \(P^2c0 + Pc1 + Pc2 t^{c3} + Pc4 + Pc5\sin(\cdot)\): the \(Pc1+Pc4\) just combines into one \(P\) coefficient; set \(c5=0\). Then match \(Pc2 t^{c3}\) to \(P t^{-2.5945}\). **Matches possible.**

6. \(Pc2(c3+t)^{c4} + Pc5\sin(\cdot)\): set \(c3=0\) to get \(Pc2 t^{c4}\), set \(c5=0\). **Matches possible.**

7. Extra additive \(c4\sin(\cdot)\) independent of \(P\): must set \(c4=0\). Then match remaining \(Pc2 t^{c3}\) etc. **Matches possible.**

8. Similar to 4/6 but additive \(c5\sin(\cdot)\) independent of \(P\): must set \(c5=0\); set \(c3=0\) to get \(t^{c4}\). **Matches possible.**

9. Has \(P c5 \exp(c6\sin(\cdot))\): this is \(P\) times a non-power function of \(t\). Only way to remove is \(c5=0\). Then left with \(Pc2(c3+t)^{c4}\) which can match with \(c3=0,c4=-2.5945\). **Matches possible.**

10. Adds \(c5 t^{c6}\) and \(c7\sin(\cdot)\) (both not multiplied by \(P\)): must set \(c5=0,c7=0\). Then as in 4/6 with \(c3=0\). **Matches possible.**

11. Entire expression is rational with denominator \(Pc1+c2\). GT is not rational in \(P\) (itŌĆÖs polynomial + separable power in \(t\)). To equal GT for all \(P\), denominator must be constant: set \(c1=0\), then denominator \(=c2\). Expression becomes a linear combination of \(P^3,P^2,P\) and \(P t^{c6}\) terms divided by constant. But GT has **no \(P^3\)**, so must set \(c0=0\). Also can combine \(P^2\) terms to match, and \(P t^{c6}\) term to match with \(c6=-2.5945\). Feasible. **Matches possible.**

12. Has extra \(P c5 (c6+t)^{c7}\sin(\cdot)\): must set \(c5=0\). Then \(Pc2(c3+t)^{c4}\) can match with \(c3=0,c4=-2.5945\). **Matches possible.**

13. Extra \(P c5 \sin(c6\log(\cdot)+c9)\): must set \(c5=0\). Remaining can match as above. **Matches possible.**

14. Extra \(c5\sin(Pc6+c7)\) depends on \(P\) non-polynomially; must set \(c5=0\). Remaining can match with shift set to 0. **Matches possible.**

15. Has rational-in-\(P\) terms \(P c4/(Pc5+c6)+c7/(Pc5+c6)\). To avoid non-polynomial \(P\) dependence, set \(c4=0,c7=0\) (or \(c5=0\) making denominator constant, but then youŌĆÖd introduce an extra \(P\) term unless also zeroed). With those zero, remaining matches. **Matches possible.**

26. \(P^2c0+Pc1+P c2(c3+t)^{c4}+P c5(c6+t)^{c7}\): can set one of the two \(P(\cdot)\) terms to 0 and use the other with shift 0 and exponent \(-2.5945\). **Matches possible.**

28. Extra \(c5\exp(Pc6)\) depends on \(P\): must set \(c5=0\). Remaining matches with shift 0. **Matches possible.**

29. Has \(c2 t^{c3}\) independent of \(P\) and log terms with \(P\): must set \(c2=0,c4=0,c7=0\). Then reduces to \(P^2c0+Pc1\) only, missing \(P t^{-2.5945}\). No remaining term can create it. **No match.**

30. Extra \(c5 t^{c6}\) independent of \(P\): set \(c5=0\). Remaining matches with shift 0. **Matches possible.**

31. Extra \(c4\exp(c5\sin(\cdots))\) independent of \(P\): set \(c4=0\). Remaining matches. **Matches possible.**

33. Extra \(P c5/(P+c6)\) rational in \(P\): must set \(c5=0\) (or force it to constant multiple of \(P\) by \(c6=0\), but then itŌĆÖs just extra \(P\) term; still removable). Then matches. **Matches possible.**
